jQuery(document).ready(function($){

    /**
     * Custom translations
     */
    /*$.urlParam = function (name) {
        var results = new RegExp('[\?&]' + name + '=([^&#]*)')
                          .exec(window.location.search);

        return (results !== null) ? results[1] || 0 : false;
    }*/
    
    $.getLocale = function () {
        var lang = document.documentElement.lang;
        if(!lang) {
            return false;
        }
        if($('body').hasClass('bodyhvg')) {
            return 'en_HVG';
        }
        if($('body').hasClass('bodysgv')) {
            return 'en_SGV';
        }
        return lang.replace('-', '_');
    }
    //console.log('locale', $.getLocale());

    $.translateLookup = function (locale, label) {
        if(!label) {
            return "";
        }

        if(!locale) {
            locale = "en_GB";
        }

        if(!customTranslationDict.hasOwnProperty(locale)) {
            locale = "en_GB";
        }
        if(!customTranslationDict[locale].hasOwnProperty(label)) {
            return "";
        }
        
        return customTranslationDict[locale][label];
    }
    //$.translateLookup($.getLocale(), 'sign_in');

    var customTranslationDict = {
        en_US: {
            sign_in: "Sign in",
            talent_community: "Talent community",
            tc_url: 'https://careers.ey.com/ey/lp/TC/f7abb34d58e4b33e/?locale=en_US',
            careers: "Careers",
        },
        en_GB: {
            sign_in: "Sign in",
            talent_community: "Talent community",
            tc_url: 'https://careers.ey.com/ey/lp/TC/0759e3395155172b/?locale=en_GB',

        },
        de_DE: {

        es_MX: {

            careers: "Careers",
        },
        fr_CA: {
            sign_in: "Se connecter",
            talent_community: "Communaut des talents",
            tc_url: 'https://careers.ey.com/ey/lp/TC/371ea27e14b25079/?locale=fr_CA',
            careers: "Carrires",
        },
        fr_FR: {
            sign_in: "S'identifier",
            talent_community: "Communaut de talents",
            tc_url: 'https://careers.ey.com/ey/lp/TC/a9b51af9cff71e9e/?locale=fr_FR',
            careers: "Carrires",
        },
        he_IL: {
            sign_in: "",
            talent_community: "",
            tc_url: 'https://careers.ey.com/ey/lp/TC/ec45f0685e48afe6/?locale=he_IL',
            careers: "",
        },
        ja_JP: {
            sign_in: "",
            talent_community: "",
            tc_url: 'https://careers.ey.com/ey/lp/TC/c995bc8d2844dbf9/?locale=ja_JP',
            careers: "Careers",
        },

        zh_CN: {

            careers: "Careers",

    /**
     * Header
     */

    // Add the additional Talent Community link to the Sign in / language modules
    $('.custom-header-signinLanguage .links').append('<div class="node"><a href="'+$.translateLookup($.getLocale(), 'tc_url')+'" title="'+$.translateLookup($.getLocale(), 'talent_community')+'" aria-label="'+$.translateLookup($.getLocale(), 'talent_community')+'">'+$.translateLookup($.getLocale(), 'talent_community')+'</a></div>');

    // Change View Profile label to Sign In
    $('.custom-header-signinLanguage .links .node.profile > .profileWidget > a').text($.translateLookup($.getLocale(), 'sign_in'));

			<script type="text/javascript">
                //<![CDATA[
                    var addthis_config = {
                        username:'addthisj2w'
                        ,ui_open_windows: true
                        ,ui_click: true
                        ,ui_508_compliant: true
                        ,data_track_clickback: false
                        ,ui_language: "es"
                        ,data_ga_property: "G-P7G5ZJ8STM"
                        ,data_ga_social: true
                    };

                    var calledsfshorturl = false;

                    $(function () {
                        var $toolbox = $('.addthis_toolbox');

                        $toolbox.mouseover(function (e) {
                            if (!calledsfshorturl) {
                                calledsfshorturl = true;
                                $(this).sfshorturl({
                                    callback:addthisCallback
                                    ,event:e
                                });
                            }
                        });

                        $toolbox.find('a.addthis_button_pinterest_share').on('click keypress', function (e) {
                            if (e.which === 13 && e.type !== 'click') {
                                $(this).click();
                                e.preventDefault();
                            }

                            if (e.type === 'click') {
                                e.preventDefault();
                            }
                        });

                        function addthisCallback(data) {
                            $(data.event.target).attr('addthis:url',data.shorturl);
                            addthis.update('share', 'url', data.shorturl);
                        }
                    });
                //]]>
			</script>

    $.getLocale = function () {
        var lang = document.documentElement.lang;
        if(!lang) {
            return false;
        }
        return lang.replace('-', '_');
    }
    //console.log('locale', $.getLocale());

    $.translateLookup = function (locale, label) {
        if(!label) {
            return "";
        }

        if(!locale) {
            locale = "en_GB";
        }

        if(!customTranslationDict.hasOwnProperty(locale)) {
            locale = "en_GB";
        }
        if(!customTranslationDict[locale].hasOwnProperty(label)) {
            return "";
        }
        
        return customTranslationDict[locale][label];
    }
    //$.translateLookup($.getLocale(), 'sign_in');

                <span class="jobdescription"><p><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">At EY, youll have the chance to build a career as unique as you are, with the global scale, support, inclusive culture and technology to become the best version of you. <p></p>
<p><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">EY is a global leader in assurance, tax, transaction and advisory services. Technology is at the heart of what we do and deliver at EY. Technology solutions are integrated in the client services we deliver and are key to our innovation as an organization. </span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Fueled by strategic investment in technology and innovation, Client Technology seeks to drive growth opportunities and solve complex business problems for our clients through building a robust platform for business and powerful product engine that are vital to innovation at scale. As part of Client Technology, youll work with technologists and business experts, blending EYs deep industry knowledge and innovative ideas with our platforms, capabilities, and technical expertise. As a catalyst for change and growth, youll be at the forefront of integrating emerging technologies from AI to Data Analytics into every corner of what we do at EY. That means more growth for you, exciting learning opportunities, career choices, and the chance to make a real impact.</span></span></p>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><b><span>The opportunity</span></b></span></span></p>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>The selected candidate will:</span></span></span></p>

<ul>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">be responsible for the JavaScript development portion of the stories for their scrum team</span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">collaborate with team tech lead, provide suggestions and direction for JavaScript development on the team</span></span></p>
	</li>
</ul>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><b><span>Your key responsibilities</span></b></span></span></p>

<p></p>

<ul>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Hands-on Development Position  70% of time coding</span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Provide Level of Effort estimates for requirements</span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Track project tasks, provide status and ensure tasks completed on schedule</span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Troubleshoot defects and code resolutions</span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Contribute to a healthy and collaborative development team with a Get it Done work ethic</span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">A commitment to excellence, best practices, and the continuous improvement of our products, code base, processes, and tools</span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Provide support for team members on JavaScript related tasks</span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Coordinate with backend developers to meet team and program goals</span></span></p>
	</li>
</ul>

<p><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><b><span>Skills and attributes for success</span></b></span></span></p>

<p></p>

<ul>
	<li style="text-align:justify">

	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Strong knowledge of one or more of: HTML, CSS and JavaScript</span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Digital Accessibility Non-Functional Requirements:</span></span></p>

	<ul>
		<li style="text-align:justify">
		<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Keyboard Access and Visual Focus: All content and functionality should be available through a keyboard. Keyboard focus should be visible and should follow a logical order through the page elements.</span></span></p>
		</li>
		<li style="text-align:justify">
		<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Page Title and Language: The page title should adequately and briefly describe the content of the page and should be different from other pages on the website. Primary language of every page and language changes should be indicated.</span></span></p>
		</li>
		<li style="text-align:justify">
		<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Headings: The page should have at least one heading. It should be marked up correctly as a heading and the heading hierarchy should be meaningful.</span></span></p>
		</li>
		<li style="text-align:justify">
		<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Images: Every image should include alt in the markup. If an image conveys information useful, then it needs alternative text. If an image is just decorative, then it should have null alt (alt="").</span></span></p>
		</li>
		<li style="text-align:justify">
		<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Contrast, Color, Appearance: The page should have a contrast ratio of at least 4.5:1 for normal-size text. Color alone should not be used to convey information.</span></span></p>
		</li>
		<li style="text-align:justify">
		<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Resizing, Magnification, Responsiveness: Users should be able to enlarge web content. The design should be responsive.</span></span></p>
		</li>
		<li style="text-align:justify">
		<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Links, Buttons, Controls, Navigation, Skip Link: Links, buttons and controls should be recognizable and coded correctly. Clear and consistent navigation options should be provided. A skip link that allows users to skip to content should be available.</span></span></p>
		</li>
		<li style="text-align:justify">
		<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Forms, Labels, Errors: Forms should be keyboard accessible. Form controls should have labels. Required fields and other instructions should be clearly indicated. Error handing should be clear and simple.</span></span></p>
		</li>
		<li style="text-align:justify">
		<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Tables and Lists: Tables should have HTML markup that indicates header cells and data cells and defines their relationship. List elements should be used for list content.</span></span></p>
		</li>
		<li style="text-align:justify">
		<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Multimedia (Audio and Video), Animation, Moving content: Captions/subtitles, transcript, and/or audio description should be provided appropriately for audio and video media. Keyboard access for media player controls, animations, carousels and other moving content should be available.</span></span></p>
		</li>
		<li style="text-align:justify">
		<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Structure, Meaning, Reading Order, Global Code: Content should be well-structured to allow efficient navigation and processing. Mark-up should be used for headings, lists, tables, etc. to better structure content. Reading order should be reflected in the code order.</span></span></p>
		</li>
		<li style="text-align:justify">
		<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Touch: Touch interactions should be supported. When phone is in scope, phone interactions should be supported.</span></span></p>
		</li>
	</ul>
	</li>
</ul>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><b><span>To qualify for the role, you must have</span></b></span></span></p>

<p></p>

<ul>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>Bachelors degree in a technical field and/or equivalent work experience</span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>10+ years of client side JavaScript experience</span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>3+ years of Angular experience</span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>7+ years of jQuery experience</span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>7+ years of RESTful application development</span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>10+ years of HTML5 experience</span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>10+ years of CSS experience </span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>Familiarity with and the ability to apply Design Patterns</span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>A firm grasp of design concepts such as Responsive Design, Progressive Enhancement, Adaptive Rendering, and Minimal Download Strategy</span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>Strong understanding on client side performance optimization techniques</span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>Experience working in Agile Development Methodologies and frameworks such as SCRUM</span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>Strong object oriented design skills and ability to articulate designs using UML diagrams </span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>Due to the nature of the effort travel may be required</span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>Self-driven to stay abreast of current technology trends</span></span></span></p>
	</li>
	<li style="text-align:justify">
	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>Proven ability to thrive under pressure</span></span></span></p>
	</li>
</ul>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><b><span>Ideally, youll also have</span></b></span></span></p>

	<p style="text-align:left"><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><span>A self-starter, independent-thinker, curious and creative person with ambition and passion</span></span></span></p>
	</li>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><b>What we offer</b></span></span></p>

<p><br>
<span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">We offer a competitive compensation package where youll be rewarded based on your performance and recognized for the value you bring to our business. In addition, our Total Rewards package includes medical and dental coverage, pension and 401(k) plans, and a wide range of paid time off options. Under our flexible vacation policy, youll decide how much vacation time you need based on your own personal circumstances. Youll also be granted time off for designated EY Paid Holidays, Winter/Summer breaks, Personal/Family Care, and other leaves of absence when needed to support your physical, financial, and emotional well-being.</span></span></p>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"> Continuous learning: Youll develop the mindset and skills to navigate whatever comes next.<br>
 Success as defined by you: Well provide the tools and flexibility, so you can make a meaningful impact, your way.<br>
 Transformative leadership: Well give you the insights, coaching and confidence to be the leader the world needs.<br>
 Diverse and inclusive culture: Youll be embraced for who you are and empowered to use your voice to help others find theirs.</span></span></p>

<p></p>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:11.0px"><span style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Working across assurance, consulting, law, strategy, tax and transactions, EY teams ask better questions to find new answers for the complex issues facing our world today.</span></span></p>

                // This code is to deal with empty e-mail strings on back button clicks to the page when first logging in.
                $(window).on( "load", function () {
                    if (''.length && !j2w.SSO.getEmail().length) {
                        $.ajax({
                            type    : 'GET',
                            url     : '/services/security/email',
                            success : function (data) {
                                if (data.email.length) {
                                    j2w.SSO.setEmail(data.email);
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }
                });

                        <script type="text/javascript">
                            //<![CDATA[
                            $(function() {
                                $('.emailsubscribe-button').click(function (e) {
                                    e.preventDefault();
                                    var $frequency = $('.subscribe-frequency').val();
                                    var rcmLoggedIn = false;
                                    var action = rcmLoggedIn ? 'alertCreate' : 'subscribe';
                                    var result = j2w.Agent.validateFrequency($frequency);
                                    if (!result.length) {
                                        j2w.TC.collectForCASWorkflow({
                                            "emailAddress": '',
                                            "action": action,
                                            "socialSrc": '',
                                            "frequency": $frequency
                                        });
                                    } else {
                                        if (j2w.Args.get('isResponsive')) {
                                            $('.frequency-error-message').html(result.concat('<br/>'));
                                            $('.frequency-error').removeClass('hidden');
                                        } else {
                                            alert(result.join('\n'));
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                            });
                            //]]>
                        </script>
